<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загружаться.html>загружа́ться</a> (32052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загружать.html>загружа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagružátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загружаться.html>загружа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagružátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">загрузи́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be booted, to be loaded
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загружаться.html>загружа́ется</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagružájetsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">loading <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually shown on a computer monitor as a "loading screen" in computer games</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">it <b>is being loaded</b></span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загружать.html>загружа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagružátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загрузивший.html>загрузи́вший</a> (11767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***загрузить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загрузить.html>загрузи́ть</a> (11767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грузить.html>грузи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gruzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузить.html>загрузи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagruzítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загружать.html>загружа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to load</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feed</li>
<li>to engage, to occupy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузить.html>загрузи́ть</a></b> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagruzítʹ</b> kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give someone a full-time job; keep someone fully occupied</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загруженный.html>загру́жен</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on óčenʹ <b>zagrúžen</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is overloaded with work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузить.html>загрузи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мощность.html>мо́щность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagruzítʹ</b> na pólnuju móščnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep running at full capacity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to boot, to load, to download</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bend someone's ear, to ramble on</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***загрузка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загрузка.html>загру́зка</a> (18456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузить.html>загрузи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagruzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузка.html>загру́зка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagrúzka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузка.html>загру́зки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузка.html>загру́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрузка.html>загру́зок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loading (of objects or cargos)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> loading, bootstrap (of computer systems)</li>
<li>download</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загрустить.html>загрусти́ть</a> (26283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***загрязнить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнить.html>загрязни́ть</a> (22551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">грязни́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grjaznítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнить.html>загрязни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagrjaznítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">грязни́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнять.html>загрязня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soil, to dirty, to make dirty, to besmirch, to litter</li>
<li>to sully, to tarnish</li>
<li>to pollute
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнить.html>загрязни́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:атмосфера.html>атмосфе́ру</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagrjaznítʹ</b> vózdux (atmosféru)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pollute the air (atmosphere)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***загрязнять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнять.html>загрязня́ть</a> (28910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнить.html>загрязни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagrjaznítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнять.html>загрязня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagrjaznjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнить.html>загрязни́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soil, to dirty, to make dirty, to besmirch, to litter</li>
<li>to pollute
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнять.html>загрязня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:атмосфера.html>атмосфе́ру</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagrjaznjátʹ</b> vózdux (atmosféru)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pollute the air (atmosphere)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***загубить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загубить.html>загуби́ть</a> (10620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губить.html>губи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загубить.html>загуби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to ruin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to waste, to ruin, to destroy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загубить.html>загуби́ть</a></b> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagubítʹ</b> čʹjú-libo žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ruin someone's life; make someone's life a misery</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загул.html>загу́л</a> (27247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загулять.html>загуля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaguljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загул.html>загу́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagúl</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загул.html>загу́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загул.html>загу́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загул.html>загу́лов</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:густеть.html>густе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gustétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зад.html>зад</a> (3058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зад.html>зад</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зад.html>за́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зад.html>зады́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зад.html>задо́в</a></b>)

***задавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ть</a> (2345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set, to assign <i>(an exercise, a lesson)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ли</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto nam ne <b>zadaváli</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It was not our homework!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ask <i>(a question)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadavátʹ</b> voprós/voprósy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask a question/questions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pose <i>(a problem)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(a dinner, a banquet)</i> to give, to throw</li>
<li><i>(a punishment)</i> to give, to administer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ть</a></b> трёпку</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadavátʹ</b> trjópku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give a thrashing, to give a dressing-down</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to preset, to specify, to assign</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задаваться.html>задава́ться</a> (12233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаваться.html>задава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаваться.html>задава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лью</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́слью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadavátʹsja</b> célʹju/mýslʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set oneself the task; make up one's mind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выучить.html>вы́учить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>zadálsja</b> célʹju výučitʹ anglíjskij jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has set himself the task of learning English</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаваться.html>задава́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadavátʹsja</b> voprósom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask oneself; wonder</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>of period, time</i> to have
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>денёк</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́лся</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nu i denjók sevódnja <b>zadálsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we have not had a day like this for a long time!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to succeed, to be a success
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поездка.html>пое́здка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>задала́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pojézdka ne <b>zadalásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the trip was not a success</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>задала́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó žiznʹ ne <b>zadalásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">life has not worked out for him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give oneself airs, to put on airs</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задавить.html>задави́ть</a> (9719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задавить.html>задави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зада́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crush <i>(to death)</i></li>
<li><i>(car)</i> to run over, to knock down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strangle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suppress, to crack down <i>(on)</i></li>
<li>to oppress, to exhaust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужда.html>нужда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задавить.html>задави́ла</a></b> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nuždá <b>zadavíla</b> kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">someone is ravaged by poverty</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́вший</a> (3023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a> (2146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>assignment, task
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:домашний.html>дома́шнее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">domášneje zadánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">homework</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>setting <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of parameters, etc., as a process</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эксперимент.html>экспериме́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́лся</a> и́з-за <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовместимый.html>несовмести́мых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:параметр.html>пара́метров</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Eksperimént provalílsja íz-za <b>zadánija</b> nesovmestímyx značénij parámetrov.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The experiment failed due to setting conflicting parameter values.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> task, mission, assignment</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задаток.html>зада́ток</a> (20970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаток.html>зада́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadátok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаток.html>зада́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаток.html>зада́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаток.html>зада́тков</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a> (3023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задавать.html>задава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set, to assign (an exercise or lesson)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>за́дали</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упражнение.html>упражне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:алгебра.html>а́лгебре</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nam <b>zádali</b> tri upražnénija po álgebre.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We were given (assigned) three exercises in algebra (as homework).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ask (a question)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadátʹ</b> voprós/voprósy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask a question/questions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pose (a problem)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give, to throw (a dinner or banquet)</li>
<li>to give, to administer (a punishment)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a></b> трёпку</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadátʹ</b> trjópku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give a thrashing, to give a dressing-down</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to preset, to specify, to assign</li></ol>

***задаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́ться</a> (16521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zadátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задаваться.html>задава́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лью</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́слью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadátʹsja</b> célʹju/mýslʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to set oneself to the task; make up one's mind</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выучить.html>вы́учить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>zadálsja</b> célʹju výučitʹ anglíjskij jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has set himself to the task of learning English</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zadátʹsja</b> voprósom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask oneself; wonder</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>of period, time</i> to have
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>денёк</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>зада́лся</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nu i denjók sevódnja <b>zadálsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we have not had a day like this for a long time!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to succeed, to be a success
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поездка.html>пое́здка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>задала́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pojézdka ne <b>zadalásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the trip was not a success</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:задаться.html>задала́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó žiznʹ ne <b>zadalásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">life has not worked out for him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give oneself airs, to put on airs</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задать.html>зада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:задачка.html>зада́чка</a> (14757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́ча</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zadáča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
